---

## Data Structure Reference

Each TODO item includes metadata in JSON format:
```json
{
  "created_at": "ISO 8601 timestamp",
  "completed_at": "ISO 8601 timestamp (only when completed)",
  "priority": "high|medium|low",
  "assigned_to": "user|agent",
  "epic": "System or subsystem name",
  "occurrence_count": "number (for recurring issues)"
}
```

## Epics

- **Cigar Management System**: All cigar inventory management features
- **Tobacco Management System**: All tobacco storage management features  
- **Hosting Management System**: Deployment, automation, and infrastructure
- **Infrastructure**: Shared infrastructure components
- **Documentation**: Documentation and guides
- **Testing**: QA and testing frameworks
- **Integration**: Third-party integrations
- **Development Environment**: Local development setup
